"processing";"ImplicitSubjectType.NOMINALIZED_VERB";"Where the processing for a purpose other than that for which the personal data have been collected is not based on the data subject’s consent or on a Union or Member State law which constitutes a necessary and proportionate measure in a democratic society to safeguard the objectives referred to in Article 23(1), the controller shall, in order to ascertain whether processing for another purpose is compatible with the purpose for which the personal data are initially collected, take into account, inter alia any link between the purposes for which the personal data have been collected and the purposes of the intended further processing.";"article6";"['personal data', 'processing', 'restriction', 'profiling', 'pseudonymisation', 'filing system', 'controller', 'processor', 'recipient', 'third party', '‘consent', '‘personal data breach', 'genetic data', 'biometric data', 'data', 'main establishment', 'representative', 'enterprise', 'group', 'supervisory authority', 'supervisory authority', 'relevant and reasoned objection', 'information society service', 'international organisation']";"{'the processing': ['controller', 'processor', 'recipient', 'third party', 'representative', 'supervisory authority', 'supervisory authority', 'information society service'], 'processing': ['controller', 'processor', 'recipient', 'third party', 'representative', 'supervisory authority', 'supervisory authority', 'information society service'], 'the intended further processing': ['controller', 'processor', 'recipient', 'third party', 'representative', 'supervisory authority', 'supervisory authority', 'information society service'], 'collected': ['controller', 'processor', 'recipient', 'third party', 'representative', 'supervisory authority', 'supervisory authority', 'information society service']}"
